# <a name="responsecode"></a><span data-ttu-id="6ee99-103">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6ee99-103">ResponseCode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6ee99-104">El elemento **ResponseCode** proporciona información de estado acerca de la solicitud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6ee99-104">The **ResponseCode** element provides status information about the request.</span></span> 
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="6ee99-105">ResponseMessage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6ee99-105">ResponseMessage</span></span>](responsemessage.md) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="6ee99-106">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6ee99-106">ResponseCode</span></span>](responsecode.md)
  
```XML
<ResponseCode/>
```

<span data-ttu-id="6ee99-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6ee99-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span></span>

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="6ee99-1480">Notas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6ee99-1480">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6ee99-1481">Este elemento no es necesario y no se incluye en todas las respuestas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6ee99-1481">This element is not required and is not included in all responses.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="6ee99-1482">El esquema que describe este elemento se encuentra en el directorio virtual IIS que hospeda los servicios Web Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6ee99-1482">The schema that describes this element is located in the IIS virtual directory that hosts Exchange Web Services.</span></span>
